msg:The hotel covers a large area and is divided into several independent buildings, mainly for business banquets. During our family of three family vacation stay, we encountered business events held here, and also encountered several weddings. Unlike the north, weddings in Nanning are all at night. Looking at the beautiful bride wearing a wedding dress on the lawn, the temperature is less than 10â„ƒ The temperature could not withstand the enthusiasm of the newlyweds.

Room and facilities: The room we stayed in had a very business-like feel when we entered it, but the room was very large. With two beds pushed together, it was quite spacious for a family. There is a terrace, and you can see the night of Nanning from a distance. It has been too cold recently. If the weather is good, it will be very comfortable to sit and drink tea on the terrace. There is a swimming pool on the ground floor of the building we live in. There are not many people, the water quality is OK, and there is a steam room.

Meal: Breakfast is served in the main building and is connected by a shuttle bus. There are a lot of Chinese and Western food. The boiled noodles include Laoyou soup base and snail noodle soup base, which taste good. The scenery outside the window is very good. There is an additional charge of 68 for children.

Location: It is a bit far from the city center and a 20-minute drive from Qingxiu Mountain. It is quite convenient for us to drive by ourselves. Parking is free during our stay.

Service: When checking in, the clerk gave the child a food bag to feed the swan, and the child was fed twice. When leaving the store, the front desk gave a cute stuffed elephant, and the service staff had a very good attitude.

On the day I checked in, I had to work, so I asked the front desk if they could help me check in early. The front desk also helped me solve the problem very well. There is also a concierge shuttle bus between each building, and the service attitude is also very good. It's not very convenient to order takeout from the surrounding area, but the hotel has Chinese and Western restaurants as well as fruit, biscuits and milk. The bar and bar are also good.
The room is very large, the balcony is also large, and the view is very good. Except that the lakeside auditorium was a little noisy because of the wedding that day, everything else was pretty good.
The air conditioning in the hotel is central air conditioning. Adjusting the temperature in the room is not very useful. It is suitable for people who are not afraid of heat, but it is a bit uncomfortable for people like me who sweat easily.
